### 3.2 矩阵的逆
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:可逆矩阵」</span>
> n阶方阵A称为可逆的,如果有n阶方阵B,使得:$AB=BA=E$,其中E为n阶单位矩阵
> >[!note] 
> >事实上,对于$A_{n\times n},B_{n\times n}$,只要有$AB=E$即可说明$A,B$互为逆矩阵
> 显然,对于任意A,适合上式的B是唯一的(如果有的话),因为$B_{1}=B_{1}E=B_{1}(AB_{2})=(B_{1}A)B_{2}=EB_{2}=B_{2}$
>  
>  如果矩阵B满足$AB=BA=E$,则B称为A的逆矩阵
>  
> 数域P上的$n\times n$矩阵称为非退化的,如果$|A|\neq0$；反之,称为退化的
> 
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:伴随矩阵」</span>
> 设$A_{ij}$是矩阵$A=\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}$中元素$a_{ij}$的代数余子式,则矩阵$A^*=\begin{bmatrix}A_{11}&A_{21}&\dots&A_{n1}\\A_{12}&A_{22}&\dots&A_{n2}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\A_{1n}&A_{2n}&\dots&A_{nn}\end{bmatrix}$称为A的伴随矩阵
> 
> 由于$AA^*=A^*A=\begin{bmatrix}d&0&\dots&0\\0&d&\dots&0\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\0&0&\dots&d\end{bmatrix}=dE,\quad(d=|A|)$
> 如果$d\neq0$,则$A\left( \frac{1}{d}A^* \right)=\left( \frac{1}{d}A^* \right)A=E$
> ==🖇️Properties:==
> (1)运算法则:$(AB)^*=B^*A^*$
> (2)$\mathrm{rank}(A^*)=\begin{cases}n,\quad\mathrm{rank}(A)=n\\1,\quad\mathrm{rank}(A)=n-1\\0,\quad\mathrm{rank}(A)<n-1\end{cases}$


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:逆的运算法则</span>
>(以下涉及的矩阵均可逆)
>数乘:$(kA)^{-1}=\frac{1}{k}A^{-1}$
>乘法:$(AB)^{-1}=B^{-1}A^{-1},\quad(ABC)^{-1}=C^{-1}B^{-1}A^{-1},\quad(ABCD)^{-1}=D^{-1}C^{-1}B^{-1}A^{-1}\dots$
>转置:$(A^T)^{-1}=(A^{-1})^T$


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
试证明:A是一个$s\times n$矩阵,如果P是$s\times s$可逆矩阵,Q是$n\times n$可逆矩阵,则$\mathrm{rank}(A)=\mathrm{rank}(PA)=\mathrm{rank}(AQ)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
令$B=PA$,则$\mathrm{rank}(B)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)$
又有$A=P^{-1}B$,则$\mathrm{rank}(A)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(B)$
于是$\mathrm{rank}(A)=\mathrm{rank}(B)=\mathrm{rank}(PA)$
另一个等式可以相仿证明
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

>[!note] 
>由于可逆矩阵可写成一系列初等矩阵的乘积,相当于对A进行初等变换,自然不改变A的秩


---


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:可逆的等价命题</span>
>n阶矩阵A可逆,与以下命题等价:
>(1)A的标准型是单位阵
>(2)A能够表示成一些初等矩阵的乘积:$A=Q_{1}Q_{2}\dots Q_{m}$
>(3)A满秩
>(4)A非退化(即$|A|\neq0$),且$A^{-1}=\frac{1}{d}A^*\quad(d=|A|\neq0)$
>(5)行向量组、列向量组线性无关



><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:逆矩阵的求法</span>
>通过初等行变换,可以将$\begin{bmatrix}A&E\end{bmatrix}\Longrightarrow \begin{bmatrix}E&A^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$
>或是通过初等列变换,可以将$\begin{bmatrix}A\\E\end{bmatrix}\Longrightarrow \begin{bmatrix}E\\A^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
$1^\circ$ 两个$s\times n$矩阵等价的充要条件是,存在可逆的n阶矩阵P和s阶矩阵Q使得:$A=PBQ$
又由于可逆矩阵的标准型是单位矩阵
$2^\circ$ 可逆矩阵总可以经过一系列初等行变换化为单位矩阵,即
$P_{n}\dots P_{1}A=E$以及$P_{n}\dots P_{1}E=A^{-1}$
这就说明,这些初等行变换在将A变为E的同时将E变为$A^{-1}$
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

>[!note] 
>由此可以延伸出,若$AB=C$,A可逆,那么$B=A^{-1}C$,就有:$\begin{bmatrix}A&C\end{bmatrix}\Longrightarrow \begin{bmatrix}E&A^{-1}C\end{bmatrix}=\begin{bmatrix}E&B\end{bmatrix}$



### 3.3 广义逆矩阵

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:广义逆矩阵」</span>
> **Lemma** 设$A$是数域P上的$s\times n$非零矩阵,则矩阵方程$AXA=A$一定有解.
> 如果$\mathrm{rank}(A)=r$,并且$A=P \begin{bmatrix}E_{r}&O\\O&O\end{bmatrix}Q$($P,Q$分别为数域P上的s阶、n阶可逆矩阵),那么该矩阵方程的通解为$X=Q^{-1}\begin{bmatrix}E_{r}&B\\C&D\end{bmatrix}$($B,C,D$分别为数域P上任意的$r\times(s-r),(n-r)\times r,(n-r)\times(s-r)$阶矩阵)
> 
>**Definition** 设$A$是数域P上的$s\times n$阶矩阵,矩阵方程$AXA=A$的每一个解都称为$A$的一个广义逆矩阵,简称广义逆,用$A^-$表示$A$的任意一个广义逆

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>

><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:非齐次线性方程组的相容性定理</span>


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:非齐次线性方程组的解的结构定理</span>

><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:齐次线性方程组的解的结构定理</span>


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:Penrose方程组</span>
>设$A$是复数域上的$s\times n$矩阵,矩阵方程组$\begin{cases}AXA=A\\XAX=X\\(AX)^*=AX\\(XA)^*=XA\end{cases}$称为$A$的Penrose方程组,它的解称为$A$的Moore-Penrose广义逆,其中$(AX)^*$表示把$AX$的每个元素取共轭复数得到的矩阵再转置
>
>如果$A$是复数域上的$s\times n$非零矩阵,$A$的Penrose方程组总是有解,并且它的解唯一.设$A=BC$,其中$B,C$分别是列满秩和行满秩矩阵,则Penrose方程组的唯一解是$X=C^*(CC^*)^{-1}(B^*B)^{-1}B^*$


### 3.4 矩阵的分块
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:矩阵的分块」</span>
> <img src="https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202412151853734.png" style="width:50%">
> 其中,$C_{pq}=\sum\limits_{k=1}^{t}A_{pk}B_{kq},\quad p=1,2,\dots t;q=1,2\dots r$
> 
> 分块矩阵相乘需要满足:
> (1)左矩阵的列组数等于右矩阵的行组数
> (2)左矩阵的每个列组所含列数等于右矩阵的相应行组所含行数




> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:准对角矩阵」</span>
> 形如$\begin{bmatrix}A_{1}&&&O\\&A_{2}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&A_{l}\end{bmatrix}$的矩阵称为准对角矩阵,其中$A_{i}(i=1,2\dots l)$是$n_{i}\times n_{i}$矩阵
> 
> 如果有两个相同分块的准对角矩阵$A=\begin{bmatrix}A_{1}&&&O\\&A_{2}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&A_{l}\end{bmatrix},B=\begin{bmatrix}B_{1}&&&O\\&B_{2}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&B_{l}\end{bmatrix}$,如果它们对应的分块是同阶的,那么显然有:
> 
> (1)乘法:$AB=\begin{bmatrix}A_{1}B_{1}&&&O\\&A_{2}B_{2}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&A_{l}B_{l}\end{bmatrix}$
> 
> (2)加法:$A+B=\begin{bmatrix}A_{1}+B_{1}&&&O\\&A_{2}+B_{2}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&A_{l}+B_{l}\end{bmatrix}$
> 
>(3)逆: $\begin{bmatrix}A_{1}&&&O\\&A_{2}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&A_{l}\end{bmatrix}^{-1}=\begin{bmatrix}A_{1}^{-1}&&&O\\&A_{2}^{-1}&&\\&&\ddots&\\O&&&A_{l}^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$


> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:分块初等矩阵」</span>
> 对单位矩阵作如下分块:$\begin{bmatrix}E_{m}&O\\O&E_{n}\end{bmatrix}$,对它进行初等变换,得到初等分块矩阵(以下对列也成立):
> (1)两行互换:$\begin{bmatrix}O&E_{n}\\E_{m}&O\end{bmatrix}$
> (2)某一行左乘(或右乘)一个非零矩阵P:$\begin{bmatrix}P&O\\O&E_{n}\end{bmatrix}$
> (3)一行乘以一个矩阵P加到另一行:$\begin{bmatrix}E_{m}&P\\O&E_{n}\end{bmatrix}$
> 同初等矩阵与初等变换的关系一样,左乘相当于进行行变换,右乘相当于进行列变换(前提是分块乘法能够进行)


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
试证明:对于矩阵$D=\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\C&B\end{bmatrix}$,其中A,B分别是k阶和r阶的可逆矩阵,C是$r\times k$矩阵,O是$k\times r$零矩阵,则它的逆矩阵为:
$D^{-1}=\begin{bmatrix}A^{-1}&O\\-B^{-1}CA^{-1}&B^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$
特别的,当$C=O$时,有$\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\O&B\end{bmatrix}^{-1}=\begin{bmatrix}A^{-1}&O\\O&B^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
$\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\O&B\end{bmatrix}^{-1}=\begin{bmatrix}A^{-1}&O\\O&B^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$是显然的
又有$\begin{bmatrix}E_{m}&O\\-CA^{-1}&E_{n}\end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\C&B\end{bmatrix}=\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\O&B\end{bmatrix}$
因此$\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\C&B\end{bmatrix}^{-1}=\begin{bmatrix}A^{-1}&O\\-B^{-1}CA^{-1}&B^{-1}\end{bmatrix}$
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>


---


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:降阶公式</span>
>设$A_{m\times m},D_{n\times n},B_{m\times n},C_{n\times m}$,则:
>1)若$A$可逆,则$\begin{vmatrix}A&B\\C&D\end{vmatrix}=|A||D-CA^{-1}B|$
>2)若$D$可逆,则$\begin{vmatrix}A&B\\C&D\end{vmatrix}=|D||A-BD^{-1}C|$
>3)若$A,D$均可逆,则$|A||D-CA^{-1}B|=|D||A-BD^{-1}C|$

>[!note] 
>记忆方法是:对于$\begin{vmatrix}A&B\\C&D\end{vmatrix}$,比如$A$可逆,则有一个因子为$|A|$,另一个因子为$A$对角的$D$减去另外三个按顺时针方向排列的乘积,其中中间的一个取逆矩阵




### 3.5 秩的运算法则
><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:秩运算定理</span>
>(以下运算中,除条件限制外,A,B不必是方阵,可相乘或相加即可)
>(1)加法:$\mathrm{rank}(A+B)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)$
>(2.0)乘法:$\mathrm{rank}(AB)\leqslant \mathrm{rank}(A)\,\&\,\mathrm{rank}(AB)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(B)$
>(2.1)(**Sylvester**)$\mathrm{rank}(AB)\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)-n\quad(A_{s\times n},B_{n\times m})$；特别的,若$AB=O$,那么$\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)\leqslant n$
>(2.2)(**Frobenius**)$\mathrm{rank}(ABC)\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(AB)+\mathrm{rank}(BC)-\mathrm{rank}(B)$
>(3)转置:$\mathrm{rank}(AA^T)=\mathrm{rank}(A^TA)=\mathrm{rank}(A)=\mathrm{rank}(A^T)$
>(4)逆:$\mathrm{rank}(A)=\mathrm{rank}(A^{-1})=n\quad(A_{n\times n})$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
(1)
令$A=\begin{bmatrix}\alpha_{1}&\alpha_{2}&\dots&\alpha_{n}\end{bmatrix},B=\begin{bmatrix}\beta_{1}&\beta_{2}&\dots&\beta_{n}\end{bmatrix}$,则$A+B=\begin{bmatrix}\alpha_{1}+\beta_{1}&\alpha_{2}+\beta_{2}&\dots&\alpha_{n}+\beta_{n}\end{bmatrix}$
设$\alpha_{i_{1}},\alpha_{i_{2}},\dots\alpha_{i_{r}}$是$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{n}$的一个极大线性无关组；$\beta_{j_{1}},\beta_{j_{2}},\dots\beta_{j_{t}}$是$\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n}$的一个极大线性无关组
则$\alpha_{1}+\beta_{1},\dots\alpha_{n}+\beta_{n}$可由向量组$\alpha_{i_{1}},\alpha_{i_{2}},\dots\alpha_{i_{r}},\beta_{j_{1}},\beta_{j_{2}},\dots\beta_{j_{t}}$
因此,$\mathrm{rank}(\alpha_{1}+\beta_{1},\dots\alpha_{n}+\beta_{n})\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(\alpha_{i_{1}},\alpha_{i_{2}},\dots\alpha_{i_{r}},\beta_{j_{1}},\beta_{j_{2}},\dots\beta_{j_{t}})\leqslant r+t$
于是$\mathrm{rank}(A+B)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)$
(2.0)
为证明$\mathrm{rank}(AB)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(B)$,令
$A=(a_{ij})_{n\times m},B=\begin{bmatrix}B_{1}\\B_{2}\\ \vdots\\B_{m}\end{bmatrix},C=AB=\begin{bmatrix}C_{1}\\C_{2}\\ \vdots\\C_{n}\end{bmatrix}$
于是$C_{i}=a_{i1}B_{1}+a_{i2}B_{2}+\dots+a_{im}B_{m},\quad i=1,2\dots n$
即$C_{i}$可以由$B_{1},B_{2},\dots B_{m}$线性表出,于是$\mathrm{rank}(AB)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(B)$
为证明$\mathrm{rank}(AB)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)$,取A的列向量即可
(2.1)
先证特殊情况:若$AB=O$,那么$\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)\leqslant n$
当$B=O$时,显然成立,不妨设$B\neq O$
令$B=\begin{bmatrix}\beta_{1}&\beta_{2}&\dots&\beta_{n}\end{bmatrix}$,则$A\beta_{i}=O$
作$AX=O$,由于$B\neq O$即有非零解,故存在基础解系,设一个基础解系为$\eta:\begin{cases}\eta_{1}\\\eta_{2}\\ \vdots\end{cases}$
由基础解系的定义,$\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n}$可由$\eta$线性表出,于是$\mathrm{rank}(B)\leqslant\mathrm{rank}(\eta)=n-\mathrm{rank}(A)$
即$\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)\leqslant n$
对于一般情况:
$0^\circ-lemma1$ 先证:对于$A_{s\times n},B_{l\times m}$,有$\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}A&O\\O&B\end{pmatrix}=\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)$
设$\mathrm{rank}(A)=r,\mathrm{rank}(B)=t$,对于$\begin{bmatrix}A&O\\O&B\end{bmatrix}$作初等行变换,得
$\begin{bmatrix}J_{r}&O\\O&O\\O&J_{t}\\O&O\end{bmatrix}$,其中$J$是阶梯型矩阵,且都是非零行
再做一次初等行变换,得$\begin{bmatrix}J_{r}&O\\O&J_{t}\\O&O\\O&O\end{bmatrix}$,显然它是阶梯型矩阵,且有r+t个非零行,因此
$\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}A&O\\O&B\end{pmatrix}=r+t=\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)$
$0^\circ-lemma2$ 再证:对于$A_{s\times n},B_{l\times m},C_{s\times m}$,有$\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}A&C\\O&B\end{pmatrix}\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)$
设$\mathrm{rank}(A)=r,\mathrm{rank}(B)=t$,则A有一个r阶非零子式$A_{1}$,B有一个t阶非零子式$B_{1}$
于是$\begin{bmatrix}A&C\\O&B\end{bmatrix}$有一个(r+t)阶子式:
$\begin{vmatrix}A_{1}&C_{1}\\O&B_{1}\end{vmatrix}=|A_{1}||B_{1}|\neq0$
因此,$\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}A&C\\O&B\end{pmatrix}\geqslant r+t=\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)$
$1^\circ$ 由引理有:
$\mathrm{rank}(E_{n})+\mathrm{rank}(AB)=n+\mathrm{rank}(AB)=\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}E_{n}&O\\O&AB\end{pmatrix}$
通过初等变换$\begin{bmatrix}E_{n}&O\\O&AB\end{bmatrix}\longrightarrow \begin{bmatrix}B&E_{n}\\O&A\end{bmatrix}$
初等变换不改变矩阵的秩,因此
$\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}E_{n}&O\\O&AB\end{pmatrix}=\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}B&E_{n}\\O&A\end{pmatrix}\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(B)+\mathrm{rank}(A)$
因此,$\mathrm{rank}(AB)\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(A)+\mathrm{rank}(B)-n$

(2.2)
即证$\mathrm{rank}(B)+\mathrm{rank}(ABC)\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(AB)+\mathrm{rank}(BC)$
初等变换后,有$\begin{bmatrix}B&O\\O&ABC\end{bmatrix}\longrightarrow \begin{bmatrix}BC&B\\O&AB\end{bmatrix}$
因此,$\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}B&O\\O&ABC\end{pmatrix}=\mathrm{rank}\begin{pmatrix}BC&B\\O&AB\end{pmatrix}$
因此$\mathrm{rank}(B)+\mathrm{rank}(ABC)\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(AB)+\mathrm{rank}(BC)$

(3)
(pf1)
$1^\circ$ 设$A_{s\times n}$,只需要证明n元齐次线性方程组$(A^TA)X=O$与$AX=O$同解,就能得出它们存在一个相同的基础解系,由解空间的维数公式:
$n-\mathrm{rank}(A^TA)=n-\mathrm{rank}(A)$
于是$\mathrm{rank}(A^TA)=\mathrm{rank}(A)$
$1.1^\circ$ 先证$AX=O$的解都是$(A^TA)=O$的解
设$\eta$是$AX=O$的任意一个解,于是$A\eta=O \Longleftrightarrow A^T(A\eta)=A^TO=O \Longleftrightarrow(A^TA)\eta=O$
即$\eta$也是$(A^TA)X=O$的一个解,由此$AX=O$的解都是$(A^TA)=O$的解
$1.2^\circ$ 再证$(A^TA)=O$的解都是$AX=O$的解
设$\delta$是$(A^TA)X=O$的任意一个解,于是$(A^TA)\delta=O \Longleftrightarrow \delta^TA^TA\delta=O \Longleftrightarrow (A\delta)^TA\delta=O$
设$(A_{s\times n}\delta_{n\times1})^T=\begin{bmatrix}c_{1}&c_{2}&\dots&c_{s}\end{bmatrix}$,则$A_{s\times n}\delta_{n\times1}=\begin{bmatrix}c_{1}\\c_{2}\\ \vdots\\c_{s}\end{bmatrix}$
于是$(A\delta)^TA\delta=O \Longleftrightarrow c_{1}^2+c_{2}^2+\dots+c_{s}^2=0 \Longleftrightarrow c_{1}=c_{2}=\dots c_{s}=0 \Longleftrightarrow A\delta=O$
于是$(A^TA)=O$只有零解,是$AX=O$的解
于是$(A^TA)X=O$与$AX=O$同解,即$\mathrm{rank}(A^TA)=\mathrm{rank}(A)$
因此$\mathrm{rank}(AA^T)=\mathrm{rank}[(A^T)^T(A^T)]=\mathrm{rank}(A^T)=\mathrm{rank}(A)$

(pf2 Binet-Cauchy不等式)




# 线性空间
## 1 数域P上的线性空间
### 1.1 线性空间
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:线性空间」</span>
> 设V是一个非空集合,P是一个数域.
> 在集合V的元素之间定义了一种代数运算,叫做加法:就是说,给出了一个法则,对于V中的任意两个元素$\alpha,\beta$,在V中都有唯一一个元素$\gamma$与之对应($(\alpha,\beta)\longmapsto\gamma$),把$\gamma$称为$\alpha,\beta$的和,记作$\gamma=\alpha+\beta$；
> 在数域P和集合V的元素之间还定义了一种运算,叫做数量乘法:就是说,对于数域P中的任一数k和V中的任一元素$\alpha$,在V中都有唯一的一个元素$\delta$与之对应($(k,\alpha)\longmapsto\delta$),把$\delta$称为$k,\alpha$的数量乘积,记为$\delta=k\alpha$；
> V称为数域P上的线性空间,如果加法和数量乘法满足以下法则($k,l\in P,\alpha,\beta\in V$):
> $1^\circ$加法交换律:$\boldsymbol{\alpha}+\boldsymbol{\beta}=\boldsymbol{\beta}+\boldsymbol{\alpha}$
> $2^\circ$加法结合律:$(\boldsymbol{\alpha}+\boldsymbol{\beta})+\boldsymbol{\gamma}=\boldsymbol{\alpha}+(\boldsymbol{\beta}+\boldsymbol{\gamma})$
> $3^\circ$零元:将元素$(0,0\dots0)$记作$\boldsymbol{0}$,有$\boldsymbol{0}+\boldsymbol{\alpha}=\boldsymbol{\alpha}+\boldsymbol{0}=\boldsymbol{\alpha}$
> $4^\circ$负元:对于$\boldsymbol{\alpha}=(a_{1},a_{2}\dots a_{n})\in P^n$,令$-\boldsymbol{\alpha}\xlongequal{def}(-a_{1},-a_{2}\dots-a_{n})\in P^n$,有$\boldsymbol{\alpha}+(-\boldsymbol{\alpha})=(-\boldsymbol{\alpha})+\boldsymbol{\alpha}=\boldsymbol{0}$ 
> $5^\circ$单位元:$1\boldsymbol{\alpha}=\boldsymbol{\alpha}$
> $6^\circ$乘法结合律:$(kl)\boldsymbol{\alpha}=k(l\boldsymbol{\alpha})$
> $7^\circ$乘法分配律:$(k+l)\boldsymbol{\alpha}=k\boldsymbol{\alpha}+l\boldsymbol{\alpha}$
> $8^\circ$第二分配律:$k(\boldsymbol{\alpha}+\boldsymbol{\beta})=k\boldsymbol{\alpha}+k\boldsymbol{\beta}$
> 
> ==🖇️Properties:==
> 1)零元素是唯一的
> 2)负元素是唯一的
> 3)$0\boldsymbol{\alpha}=\boldsymbol{0};k\boldsymbol{0}=\boldsymbol{0};(-1)\boldsymbol{\alpha}=-\boldsymbol{\alpha}$
> 4)若$k\boldsymbol{\alpha}=\boldsymbol{0}$,那么$k=0$或$\boldsymbol{\alpha}=\boldsymbol{0}$
> 
> 线性空间中的元素也称为向量,线性空间有时也称为向量空间

>[!note] 
>线性空间定义中的加法交换律可以由定义中的其它运算法则推出


>[!example] 
>1)数域P上一元多项式环$P[x]$,按照通常的多项式加法和数与多项式的乘法,构成一个数域P上的线性空间.如果只考虑其中次数小于n的多项式,在添上零多项式也构成数域P上的一个线性空间,记为$P[x]_{n}$
>2)元素属于数域P的$m\times n$矩阵,按照矩阵的加法和与数的数量乘法,构成数域P上的一个线性空间,用$P^{m\times n}$表示(或$M_{m\times n}(P)$)
>3)数域P上的n阶实对称(反称、上三角形)矩阵,按照矩阵的加法和与数的数量乘法,构成数域P上的一个线性空间
>4)全体正实数$\mathbb{R}^+$,加法和数量乘法定义为:$a\oplus b=ab;k\circ a=a^k$,构成数域$\mathbb{R}$上的一个线性空间
>5)全体实函数,按照函数的加法和数与函数的数量乘法,构成数域$\mathbb{R}$上的一个线性空间
>6)数域P按照自身的加法和乘法,就构成一个自身的线性空间


### 1.2 维数、基与坐标
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:维数」</span>
> 如果在数域P上的线性空间V中有n个线性无关的向量,但是没有更多数目的线性无关的向量,那么V就称为n维的,记作$\dim_{P}V=n$,简记为$\dim V=n$
> 如果在V中可以找到任意多个线性无关的向量,那么V就称为无限维的,记为$\dim V =\infty$
> 
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:基与坐标」</span>
> 在n维线性空间V中, n个线性无关的向量$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$称为V的一组基
> 设$\alpha$是V中的任一向量,于是$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n},\alpha$线性相关,因此$\alpha$可以由$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$线性表出,即$\alpha=a_{1}\varepsilon_{1}+a_{2}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots+a_{n}\varepsilon_{n}$,其中$a_{1},a_{2},\dots a_{n}$是被向量$\alpha$和基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$唯一确定的,这组数就称为$\alpha$在基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$下的坐标,记为$(a_{1},a_{2},\dots a_{n})$
> 
> 关于基有如下定理:
> 如果在线性空间V中有n个线性无关的向量$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$,且V中的任一向量都可以经它们线性表出,那么V是n维的,而$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$就是V的一组基

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
既然$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性无关.那么V的维数至少是n
为了证明V是n维的,只需证明V中任意$n+1$个向量是线性相关的即可
设$\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n},\beta_{n+1}$是V中任意$n+1$个向量,它们可以经$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性表出
假设它们线性无关,就有$n+1\leqslant n$,矛盾
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

>[!important] 
>在向量代数中的一些命题可以移植到线性空间中:
>在数域P上的线性空间V中
>1)向量$\beta$可以由$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性表出,那么表出方法唯一的充要条件是:$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性无关
>2)设向量组$\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{r}$可以由$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s}$线性表出:
>	- a.若$\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{r}$线性无关,那么$r\leqslant s$
>	- b.若$r>s$,那么$\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{r}$线性相关
>3)若$\dim V=n$,那么V中任意n个线性无关的向量都是V的一个基
>4)若V中的每一个向量都可以由向量组$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性表出,那么$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{n}$是V中的一个基
>5)若$\dim V=n$,那么V中任意一个线性无关的向量组都可以扩充成V的一个基

>[!example] 常见线性空间的基与维数
>1)$P^{m\times n}$:一个基是$\{ E_{ij}|1\leqslant i\leqslant m,1\leqslant j\leqslant n \}$,维数为$mn$
>2)数域$P$上所有n阶对称矩阵组成的线性空间:一个基是$E_{11},E_{22},\dots E_{nn},E_{12}+E_{21},E_{13}+E_{31},\dots$,维数为$\frac{n(n+1)}{2}$
>3)


>[!note] 
>基也可定义为:
>设线性空间$V$中的一个向量组$S$满足:
>1)$S$本身是线性无关的
>2)$V$中任意一个向量均可由$S$中的有限多个向量线性表出
>那么称$S$是$V$的一个基
>
>任一域上的任一线性空间都存在一个基,证明需要用到偏序集和Zorn引理
>
>一个基中向量的个数称为线性空间的维数

### 1.3 基变换与坐标变换
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:基变换与坐标变换」</span>
> 设$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$和$\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}'$是n维线性空间V中的两组基,且
> $\begin{cases}\varepsilon_{1}'=a_{11}\varepsilon_{1}+a_{21}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots a_{n1}\varepsilon_{n}\\ \varepsilon_{2}'=a_{12}\varepsilon_{1}+a_{22}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots a_{n2}\varepsilon_{n}\\\dots\\ \varepsilon_{n}'=a_{1n}\varepsilon_{1}+a_{2n}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots a_{nn}\varepsilon_{n}\end{cases}\quad(1)$
> 设向量$\xi$在这两组基下的坐标分别是$(x_{1},x_{2},\dots x_{n}),(x_{1}',x_{2}',\dots x_{n}')$,
> 为了找出它们之间的关系,记$\xi=x_{1}\varepsilon_{1}+x_{2}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots x_{n}\varepsilon_{n}=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{pmatrix}$,这是一种形式写法,给出这种写法的一些运算规律
> ==🖇️Properties:==
> 设$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$和$\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{n}$是V中的两个向量组,$A=(a_{ij}),B=(b_{ij})$是两个$n\times n$矩阵,那么:
> 1)$((\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})A)B=(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})(AB)$
> 2)$(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})A+(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})B=(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})(A+B)$
> 3)$(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})A+(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{n})A=(\alpha_{1}+\beta_{1},\alpha_{2}+\beta_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}+\beta_{n})A$
> 
> 那么,$(1)$就可以写作$(\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}')=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}$
> 矩阵$A=\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}$称为由基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$到$\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}'$的<span style="background:#d2cbff">过渡矩阵</span>,它是<span style="background:#d2cbff">可逆的</span>
> 
> 给出以下定理:
> $\begin{bmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{bmatrix}=\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{bmatrix}$或$\begin{bmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{bmatrix}=\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}^{-1}\begin{bmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{bmatrix}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
由于$\xi=x_{1}\varepsilon_{1}+x_{2}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots x_{n}\varepsilon_{n}=x_{1}'\varepsilon_{1}'+x_{2}'\varepsilon_{2}'+\dots x_{n}'\varepsilon_{n}'$,即
$\xi=(\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}')\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{pmatrix}$
由于$(\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}')=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}$,代入有:
$\xi=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{pmatrix}$
与$\xi=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{pmatrix}$进行比较:
移项,有:
$(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})(\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{pmatrix}-\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{pmatrix})=0$
设$\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{pmatrix}-\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}\begin{pmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{pmatrix}=\begin{pmatrix}k_{1}\\k_{2}\\ \vdots\\k_{n}\end{pmatrix}$
则即为$(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{pmatrix}k_{1}\\k_{2}\\ \vdots\\k_{n}\end{pmatrix}=k_{1}\varepsilon_{1}+k_{2}\varepsilon_{2}+k_{n}\varepsilon_{n}=0$
由于$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$是V的一组基,即线性无关,于是$k_{1}=k_{2}=\dots=k_{n}=0$,于是
$\begin{bmatrix}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\ \vdots\\x_{n}\end{bmatrix}=\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&\dots&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}\begin{bmatrix}x_{1}'\\x_{2}'\\ \vdots\\x_{n}'\end{bmatrix}$

>[!note] 
>最后一步也可以借助如下命题:
>设$\beta$可以由$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性表出,那么表出方法唯一的充要条件是:$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$线性无关


>[!caution] 
>注意$X=CY$是由$X$到$Y$的线性替换,而$(\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}')=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n})\begin{bmatrix}a_{11}&a_{12}&\dots&a_{1n}\\a_{21}&a_{22}&\dots&a_{2n}\\ \vdots&\vdots&&\vdots\\a_{n1}&a_{n2}&&a_{nn}\end{bmatrix}$中的$A$是由基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots \varepsilon_{n}$到$\varepsilon_{1}',\varepsilon_{2}',\dots \varepsilon_{n}'$的过渡矩阵


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem</span>
>设$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$是线性空间$V$的一个基,且有$(\eta_{1},\eta_{2},\dots \eta_{n})=(\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n})A$,则$\eta_{1},\eta_{2},\dots \eta_{n}$是$V$的一个基当且仅当$A$是可逆矩阵

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506160952311.png)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
设$C$是数域$P$上的n阶循环位移矩阵,即$C=\begin{bmatrix}\varepsilon_{n},\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n-1}\end{bmatrix}$.试证:在线性空间$P^{n\times n}$中,$E,C,C^2,\dots C^{n-1}$线性无关

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>

1)用$M_{n}^0(F)$表示域$F$上所有迹为0的n阶矩阵组成的集合

## 2 子空间
### 2.1 线性子空间
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:子空间」</span>
> 数域P上线性空间V的一个非空子集合W称为V的一个线性子空间(简称子空间),如果W对于V的两种运算也构成数域P上的线性空间
> 
> 在线性空间中,零子空间和线性空间本身这两个子空间叫做平凡子空间,其它的称为非平凡子空间
> 
> <span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:子空间判别法</span>
> 设W是V的非空子集合,那么W是V的一个线性子空间,当且仅当:
> 1)若$\alpha\in W$,则$k\alpha\in W\quad(k\in P)$
> 2)若$\alpha,\beta\in W$,则$\alpha+\beta\in W$

>[!example] 
>1)在线性空间中,单个零向量组成的子集是一个线性子空间,它叫做零子空间
>2)在全体实函数组成的空间中,所有的实系数多项式组成一个子空间
>3)$P[x]_{n}$是线性空间$P[x]$的子空间
>4)线性空间$P^n$中,齐次线性方程组$\begin{cases}a_{11}x_{1}+a_{12}x_{2}+\dots+a_{1n}x_{n}=0\\a_{21}x_{1}+a_{22}x_{2}+\dots+a_{2n}x_{n}=0\\\quad\vdots\qquad\quad\vdots \qquad\quad\quad\quad\vdots\\a_{s1}x_{1}+a_{s2}x_{2}+\dots+a_{sn}x_{n}=0\end{cases}$的全部解向量组成一个子空间,这个子空间叫做齐次线性方程组的解空间.非齐次或非线性一般不满足





---

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:张成的子空间」</span>
> 设$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}$是线性空间V中的一组向量,它们所有可能的线性组合$k_{1}\alpha_{1}+k_{2}\alpha_{2}+\dots+k_{r}\alpha_{r}$所成的集合是非空的,而且对于两种运算封闭,因而是V的一个子空间,这个子空间叫做由$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}$张成的子空间,记为$L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r})$或$\langle\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}\rangle$

>[!note] 
>事实上,$L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r})$就是包含$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}$的最小的子空间

> ==🖇️Properties:==
> 1)两个向量组张成相同的子空间的充分必要条件是这两个向量组等价
> 2)$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}$的一个极大线性无关组就是$L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r})$的一个基,也就是说$L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r})$的维数等于$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}$的秩

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161003075.png)


---
<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
证明:域$F$上n维线性空间$F^{n}$的任一子空间是域$F$上某个齐次线性方程组的解空间

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506160958630.png)

### 2.2 子空间的交与和
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:子空间的交」</span>
>如果$V_{1},V_{2}$是线性空间$V$的两个子空间,那么它们的交$V_{1}\cap V_{2}$也是$V$的子空间
>
>==🖇️Properties:==
>**交换律** $V_{1}\cap V_{2}=V_{2}\cap V_{1}$
>**结合律** $(V_{1}\cap V_{2})\cap V_{3}=V_{1}\cap(V_{2}\cap V_{3})$
>
>可扩展到多个子空间的交

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:子空间的和」</span>
> 设$V_{1},V_{2}$是线性空间$V$的子空间,所谓$V_{1},V_{2}$的和是指所有能表示成$\alpha_{1}+\alpha_{2}\quad(\alpha_{1}\in V_{1},\alpha_{2}\in V_{2})$的向量组成的子集合,记作$V_{1}+V_{2}$
> 
> 如果$V_{1},V_{2}$是$V$的线性子空间,那么它们的和$V_{1}+V_{2}$也是$V$的线性子空间

>[!note] 
>$V_{1}+V_{2}$是包含$V_{1}\cup V_{2}$的最小子空间

> ==🖇️Properties:==
> **交换律** $V_{1}+V_{2}=V_{2}+V_{1}$
> **结合律** $(V_{1}+V_{2})+V_{3}=V_{1}+(V_{2}+V_{3})$

>[!note] 
>关于子空间的交与和,有以下结论:
>1)设$V_{1},V_{2},W$都是子空间,那么如果$W\subset V_{1},V_{2}\Longrightarrow W\subset V_{1}\cap V_{2};\quad W\supset V_{1},V_{2}\Longrightarrow W\supset V_{1}+V_{2}$
>2)对于子空间$V_{1},V_{2}$,以下结论等价:$V_{1}\subset V_{2};\quad V_{1}\cap V_{2}=V_{1};\quad V_{1}+V_{2}=V_{2}$

---

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
设$V_{1},V_{2}$都是域$F$上线性空间$V$的两个真子空间(即$V_{i}\neq V(i=1,2)$),证明:$V_{1}\cup V_{2}\neq V$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161013241.png)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
在数域$K$上的线性空间$K^4$中,$V_{1}=L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\alpha_{3}),V_{2}=L(\beta_{1},\beta_{2})$,其中:
$\begin{cases}\alpha_{1}=\begin{pmatrix}1&2&1&0\end{pmatrix}\\\alpha_{2}=\begin{pmatrix}-1&1&1&1\end{pmatrix}\\\alpha_{3}=\begin{pmatrix}0&3&2&1\end{pmatrix}\end{cases},\begin{cases}\beta_{1}=\begin{pmatrix}2&-1&0&1\end{pmatrix}\\\beta_{2}=\begin{pmatrix}1&-1&3&7\end{pmatrix}\end{cases}$
分别求$V_{1}+V_{2},V_{1}\cap V_{2}$的一个基与维数

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Solution :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161020223.png)

>[!important] 
>求$V_{1}+V_{2}$的一个基时,可以将它们写在一起$A=\begin{pmatrix}\alpha_{1}&\alpha_{2}&\dots&\beta_{1}&\beta_{2}&\dots\end{pmatrix}$,然后化成简化行阶梯形矩阵,就可以得到$V_{1}+V_{2}$的一个基
>
>求$V_{1}\cap V_{2}$的一个基时,$x_{1}\alpha_{1}+x_{2}\alpha_{2}+x_{3}\alpha_{3}\in V_{1}\cap V_{2}$当且仅当存在$y_{1}'\beta_{1}+y_{2}'\beta_{2}$使得$x_{1}\alpha_{1}+x_{2}\alpha_{2}+x_{3}\alpha_{3}=y'_{1}\beta_{1}+y'_{2}\beta_{2}$也可以写成$x_{1}\alpha_{1}+x_{2}\alpha_{2}+x_{3}\alpha_{3}+y_{1}\beta_{1}+y_{2}\beta_{2}=0$,列出方程组,求得基础解系与全部解即得一个基
>![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161035330.png)




### 2.3 维数公式
><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:张成子空间的和公式</span>
>在线性空间$V$中,有:$L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{s})+L(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{t})=L(\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t})$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
只需证明:
$\forall x\in L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{s}),\forall y\in  L(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{t}),x+y\in L(\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t})$
$\forall z\in L(\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t}),\exists x,y(x+y=z):x\in  L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{s}),y\in L(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{t})$
即可
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:子空间的维数公式</span>
>设$V_{1},V_{2}$是线性空间$V$的两个子空间,有$\dim(V_{1})+\dim(V_{2})=\dim(V_{1}+V_{2})+\dim(V_{1}\cap V_{2})$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
设$\dim(V_{1})=n_{1},\dim(V_{2}=n_{2}),\dim(V_{1}\cap V_{2})=m$
取$V_{1}\cap V_{2}$的一组基$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m}$
若$m=0$,基为空集,下面的讨论中$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m}$不出现,讨论同样进行.
由任意一组线性无关的向量可扩充成一组基可知:
可以扩充成$V_{1}$的一组基$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m}$
可以扩充成$V_{2}$的一组基$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m}$
只需证明:$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m}$是$V_{1}+V_{2}$的一组基,结论自明
由于$V_{1}=L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m}),V_{2}=L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m})$
因此有张成子空间的和公式,$V_{1}+V_{2}=L(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m})$
只需证明$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m}$线性无关即可
假设有$k_{1}\alpha_{1}+\dots k_{m}\alpha_{m}+p_{1}\beta_{1}+\dots p_{n_{1}-m}\beta_{n_{1}-m}+q_{1}\gamma_{1}+\dots q_{n_{2}-m}\gamma_{n_{2}-m}=0$
令$\alpha=k_{1}\alpha_{1}+\dots k_{m}\alpha_{m}+p_{1}\beta_{1}+\dots p_{n_{1}-m}\beta_{n_{1}-m}=-q_{1}\gamma_{1}-\dots q_{n_{2}-m}\gamma_{n_{2}-m}$
由左侧等式,$\alpha\in V_{1}$;由右侧等式$\alpha\in V_{2}$.于是$\alpha\in V_{1}\cap V_{2}$,即$\alpha$可由$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{m}$线性表出
令$\alpha=l_{1}\alpha_{1}+\dots l_{m}\alpha_{m}$,则$l_{1}\alpha_{1}+\dots l_{m}\alpha_{m}+q_{1}\gamma_{1}+\dots q_{n_{2}-m}\gamma_{n_{2}-m}=0$
由于$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m}$线性无关,因此$l_{1}=\dots=l_{m}=q_{1}=\dots q_{n_{2}-m}=0$
因此$\alpha=0$,从而$k_{1}\alpha_{1}+\dots k_{m}\alpha_{m}+p_{1}\beta_{1}+\dots p_{n_{1}-m}\beta_{n_{1}-m}=0$,由于$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m}$线性无关,因此$k_{1}=\dots k_{m}=p_{1}=\dots p_{n_{1}-m}=0$
这就证明了$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{m},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{n_{1}-m},\gamma_{1},\dots\gamma_{n_{2}-m}$线性无关
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

### 2.4 子空间的直和
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:直和」</span>
> 设$V_{1},V_{2}$是线性空间$V$的两个子空间,如果和$V_{1}+V_{2}$中的每一个向量$\alpha$的分解式$\alpha=\alpha_{1}+\alpha_{2}\quad(\alpha_{1}\in V_{1},\alpha_{2}\in V_{2})$是唯一的,这个和就称为直和,记为$V_{1}\oplus V_{2}$

><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:和是直和的充要条件</span>
>和$V_{1}+V_{2}$是直和的充要条件是:
>1)零向量的分解式唯一,即$\boldsymbol{0}=\boldsymbol{0}+\boldsymbol{0}$
>2)$V_{1}\cap V_{2}=\{\boldsymbol{0}\}$
>3)$\dim(V_{1}+ V_{2})=\dim(V_{1})+\dim(V_{2})$
>3')$V_{1}$的一个基与$V_{2}$的一个基合起来是$V_{1}+V_{2}$的一个基
>
>以上均可推导到多个子空间的直和的情况

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
**1)**
$\Longrightarrow$
由定义,必要性是显然的
$\Longleftarrow$
设$\alpha\in V_{1}+V_{2}$,假设它有两个分解式$\alpha=\alpha_{1}+\alpha_{2}=\beta_{1}+\beta_{2},\quad\alpha_{i},\beta_{i}\in V_{i},i=1,2$
于是$(\alpha_{1}-\beta_{1})+(\alpha_{2}-\beta_{2})=0$,其中$\alpha_{i}-\beta_{i}\in V_{i}(i=1,2)$
由定理条件$\alpha_{i}-\beta_{i}=0(i=1,2)$
即分解式唯一
**2)**
$\Longrightarrow$
任取$\alpha\in V_{1}\cap V_{2}$,于是零向量可以表示为$0=\alpha+(-\alpha),\alpha\in V_{1},-\alpha\in V_{2}$
由于是直和,故$\alpha=-\alpha=0$,这就是$V_{1}\cap V_{2}=\{\boldsymbol{0}\}$

$\Longleftarrow$
假设有$\alpha_{1}+\alpha_{2}=0,\quad\alpha_{i}\in V_{i}(i=1,2)$
那么$\alpha_{1}=-\alpha_{2}\in V_{1}\cap V_{2}$
由假设$\alpha_{1}=\alpha_{2}=0$,即零向量分解式唯一,$V_{1}+V_{2}$是直和

**3)**
由维数公式立即可得结论
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>
3')
3'到3是显然的,下面证明3到3'
由于$\dim(V_{1}+ V_{2})=\dim(V_{1})+\dim(V_{2})$,在$V_{1},V_{2}$中各取一个基$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{s};\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{t}$,则
$V_{1}+V_{2}=L(\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s})+L(\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t})=L(\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t})$
由条件得$\dim(V_{1}+V_{2})=s+t$,又由于$V_{1}+V_{2}$中的每个向量都可以由$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t}$线性表出,因而$\alpha_{1},\dots\alpha_{s},\beta_{1},\dots\beta_{t}$是$V_{1}+V_{2}$的一个基
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>


> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:补空间」</span>
> 设$V_{1},V_{2}$是线性空间$V$的两个子空间,如果$V_{1}+V_{2}=V$且$V_{1}\oplus V_{2}=V$,此时称$V_{2}$是$V_{1}$的一个补空间
> 
> ==🖇️Properties:==
> 对于线性空间$V$,它的每一个子空间$W$都有补空间

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>


---
<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
设$A$是数域$P$上的一个n阶矩阵,试证:数域$P$上所有与$A$可交换的矩阵组成的集合是$P^{n\times n}$的一个子空间,将它记为$C(A)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506160957754.png)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
设$V$是域$F$上的线性空间,$V_{1},V_{2}$都是$V$的子空间,$V_{11},V_{12}$都是$V_{1}$的子空间.试证:如果$V=V_{1}\oplus V_{2},V_{1}=V_{11}\oplus V_{12}$,那么$V=V_{11}\oplus V_{12}\oplus V_{2}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161058517.png)
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

## 3 同构
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:同构」</span>
> 数域P上的两个线性空间$V,V'$称为同构的,如果由$V$到$V'$有一个双射$\sigma$,满足:
> 1)$\sigma(\alpha+\beta)=\sigma(\alpha)+\sigma(\beta)$
> 2)$\sigma(k\alpha)=k\sigma(\alpha)$
> 其中,$\alpha,\beta$是任意向量,$k$是P中任意数,这样的映射称为同构映射
> 
> 同构映射$\sigma$有以下性质
> ==🖇️Properties:==
> 1)零元:$\sigma(0)=0$
> 2)负元:$\sigma(-\alpha)=-\sigma(\alpha)$
> 3)线性组合:$\sigma(k_{1}\alpha_{1}+\dots k_{n}\alpha_{n})=k_{1}\sigma(\alpha_{1})+\dots k_{n}\sigma(\alpha_{n})$
> 4)线性相关:$V$中向量组$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{r}$线性相关的充要条件是它们的像$\sigma(\alpha_{1}),\sigma(\alpha_{2}),\dots\sigma(\alpha_{n})$线性相关
> 5)维数:如果$V_{1}$是$V$的一个线性子空间,那么$V_{1}$在$\sigma$下的像集合$\sigma(V_{1})=\{ \sigma(\alpha)|\alpha\in V_{1} \}$是$\sigma(V)$的子空间,并且$\dim(V_{1})=\dim(\sigma(V_{1}))$
> 6)逆映射:同构映射的逆映射还是同构映射
> 7)乘积:两个同构映射的乘积还是同构映射

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
4)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161059460.png)
6)7)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161100859.png)


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem</span>
>数域P上两个有限维线性空间同构的充要条件是它们有相同的维数

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
$\Longrightarrow$ 若$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$是$V$的一个基,那么$\sigma(\alpha_{1}),\sigma(\alpha_{2}),\dots\sigma(\alpha_{n})$是$V'$的一个基
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161103139.png)
$\Longleftarrow$
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161104804.png)


---

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
设$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$是n维线性空间$V$的一组基,且$(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{s})=(\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n})A_{n\times s}$,试证:$\mathrm{rank}(\beta_{1},\beta_{2},\dots\beta_{s})=\mathrm{rank}(A)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161105187.png)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161107507.png)


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
设$V_{1},V_{2}$都是域$F$上线性空间$V$的子空间,$\sigma$是$V$到自身的一个同构映射,试证:如果$V=V_{1}\oplus V_{2}$,那么$V=\sigma(V_{1})\oplus\sigma(V_{2})$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
$1^\circ$ 先证$V=\sigma(V_{1})+\sigma(V_{2})$
任取$\alpha\in V$,由于$\sigma$是满射,故必然存在$\beta\in V,s.t.\alpha=\sigma(\beta)$
由于$V=V_{1}+V_{2}$,因此存在$\beta_{1}\in V_{1},\beta_{2}\in V_{2},s.t.\beta=\beta_{1}+\beta_{2}$
从而$\alpha=\sigma(\beta)=\sigma(\beta_{1}+\beta_{2})=\sigma(\beta_{1})+\sigma(\beta_{2})\in\sigma(V_{1})+\sigma(V_{2})$
因此$V\subset\sigma(V_{1})+\sigma(V_{2})$,于是$V=\sigma(V_{1})+\sigma(V_{2})$
$2^\circ$ 再证$\sigma(V_{1})\cap\sigma(V_{2})=\{ 0 \}$
任取$\gamma \in\sigma(V_{1})\cap\sigma(V_{2})$,则$\gamma \in\sigma(V_{1})$且$\gamma \in\sigma(V_{2})$
于是$\exists\delta_{1}\in V_{1},\delta_{2}\in V_{2},s.t.\gamma=\sigma(\delta_{1})=\sigma(\delta_{2})$
由于$\sigma$是单射,因此$\delta_{1}=\delta_{2}$,于是$\delta_{1}\in V_{1}\cap V_{2}$
由于$V_{1}+V_{2}$是直和,因此$V_{1}\cap V_{2}=\{ 0 \}$,从而$\delta_{1}=0$
于是$\gamma=\sigma(\delta_{1})=\sigma(0)=0$,从而$\sigma(V_{1})\cap\sigma(V_{2})=\{ 0 \}$
因此$V=\sigma(V_{1})\oplus\sigma(V_{2})$
<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
若$A,B$都是域$F$上的n阶矩阵,若$A\sim B$,则$C(A)\cong C(B)$,从而$\dim C(A)=\dim C(B)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161108034.png)

>[!note] 
>本题给出了求$C(A)$的基本方法:先求出$A$的相似标准形$B$,然后求$C(B)$,最后便得出$\dim C(A)=\dim C(B)$.知道$C(A)$的维数为$r$后,只要在$C(A)$中找出$r$个线性无关的矩阵,即可得出$C(A)$的一个基.通常可以考虑$E,A,A^2,\dots A^{r-1}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 4 </span>
求$C(A)$的维数和一个基
1)设$A$是数域$K$上的三阶矩阵,且$A$有n个不同的特征值
2)设$A=\begin{bmatrix*}1&0&4\\0&1&2\\0&1&2\end{bmatrix*}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Solution :</span>
1)
存在可逆矩阵$P$使得$P^{-1}AP=\mathrm{diag}\{ \lambda_{1},\lambda_{2},\dots\lambda_{n} \}=:D$
由于与主对角元两两不等的对角矩阵可交换的矩阵一定是对角矩阵,且反之亦然,因此$C(D)$是有数域$K$上的所有n阶对角矩阵组成的集合
由于任一n阶对角矩阵可以表示成$\mathrm{diag}\{ b_{1},b_{2},\dots b_{n} \}=b_{1}E_{11}+b_{2}E_{22}+\dots b_{n}E_{nn}$,且$E_{11},E_{22},\dots E_{nn}$线性无关,因此$E_{11},E_{22},\dots E_{nn}$是$C(D)$的一个基,从而$\dim C(D)=n$
由上题得,$\dim C(A)=\dim C(D)=n$,$C(A)$的一个基为$PE_{11}P^{-1},PE_{22}P^{-1},\dots PE_{nn}P^{-1}$
2)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161125032.png)


## 4 商空间


# 线性映射
## 1 线性映射及其计算
### 1.1 线性映射的定义
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:线性映射」</span>
> 设$V,V'$是数域P上的两个线性空间,$V$到$V'$的一个映射如果$\mathcal{A}$保持加法运算和数量乘法运算,即:
> $\mathcal{A}(\alpha+\beta)=\mathcal{A}(\alpha)+\mathcal{A}(\beta),\quad \forall\alpha,\beta\in V$
> $\mathcal{A}(k\alpha)=k\mathcal{A}(\alpha),\quad \forall\alpha\in V,\forall k\in P$
> 那么称$\mathcal{A}$是$V$到$V'$的一个线性映射
> 
> ==🖇️Properties:==
> 1)(零元)$\mathcal{A}0=0'$,其中$0'$是$V'$的零向量
> 2)(负元)$\mathcal{A}(-\alpha)=-\mathcal{A}(\alpha),\forall\alpha\in V$
> 3)(线性组合)$\mathcal{A}(k_{1}\alpha_{1}+k_{2}\alpha_{2}+\dots k_{s}\alpha_{s})=k_{1}\mathcal{A}\alpha_{1}+k_{2}\mathcal{A}\alpha_{2}+\dots k_{s}\mathcal{A}\alpha_{s}$
> 4)(线性相关)$\mathcal{A}$将$V$中线性相关的向量组$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{s}$映射为$V'$中线性相关的向量组$\mathcal{A}(\alpha_{1}),\mathcal{A}(\alpha_{2}),\dots \mathcal{A}(\alpha_{s})$
> >[!caution] 
> >但是,$\mathcal{A}$可能将$V$中线性无关的向量组映射成$V'$中线性相关的向量组,例如零映射.这与同构映射不同,同构映射严格保持线性相关性/无关性.
> 
> 线性空间$V$到自身的线性映射通常称为$V$上的<span style="background:#d2cbff">线性变换</span>
> 数域P上线性空间$V$到P上的线性映射称为$V$上的<span style="background:#d2cbff">线性函数</span>

>[!tip]
$\mathcal{A}(\alpha)$也可以写为$\mathcal{A}\alpha$

>[!tip] 
>域自然构成其自身上的一维线性空间,故线性函数的定义是相容的.

>[!example] 线性变换的例子
>**转轴变换** 平面上的向量构成实数域$\mathbb{R}$上的二维线性空间.把平面围绕坐标原点逆时针方向旋转$\theta$角,就是一个线性变换,用$\mathcal{P}_{\theta}$表示.类似的空间中绕轴的旋转也是一个线性变换
>
>**内射影** 设$\alpha$是空间中一个固定的非零向量,把每个向量$\zeta$变换到它在$\alpha$上的内射影的变换也是一个线性变换,用$\Pi_{\alpha}$表示,即$\Pi_{\alpha}(\zeta)= \frac{(\alpha,\zeta)}{(\alpha,\alpha)}\alpha$
>
>**恒等变换(单位变换)** $\mathcal{E}(\alpha)=\alpha,\alpha\in V$
>**零变换** $\mathcal{0}(\alpha)=0$ 
>**数乘变换** 设$V$是数域P上的线性空间,$k\in P$,则有线性变换$\mathcal{K}(\alpha)=k\alpha,k\in P$.当$k=1$时即为恒等变换,当$k=0$时即为零变换


### 1.2 线性映射存在性与唯一性
><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:线性映射的存在性与唯一性定理</span>
>**唯一性** 设$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$是线性空间$V$的一组基,如果线性映射$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$在这组基上的作用相同,即$\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{i}=\mathcal{B}\varepsilon_{i},\quad(i=1,2,\dots n)$,那么$\mathcal{A}=\mathcal{B}$
>>[!note] 
>>$\mathcal{A}$和$\mathcal{B}$相同的意义是它们对于任意一个向量的作用都相同,此性质将其弱化为对基的作用相同即可
>
>**存在性** 设$V,V'$都是数域P上的线性空间,且$V$是有限维的.在$V$中取一个基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$;$V'$中任意取定n个向量$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$(它们可以相同).则一定存在一个线性变换$\mathcal{A},s.t.\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{i}=\alpha_{i},\quad(i=1,2,\dots n)$
>
>**存在性与唯一性定理**
>设$V,V'$都是数域P上的线性空间,且$V$是有限维的.
>在$V$中取一个基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$;$V'$中任意取定n个向量$\alpha_{1},\alpha_{2},\dots\alpha_{n}$(它们可以相同).令:
>$\mathcal{A}:\qquad\begin{matrix}V\longrightarrow V'\\ \xi=\sum\limits_{i=1}^{n}x_{i}\varepsilon_{i}\longmapsto \sum\limits_{i=1}^{n}x_{i}\alpha_{i}\end{matrix}$
>则$\mathcal{A}$是$V$到$V'$的一个线性映射,且$\mathcal{A}$满足且唯一满足$\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{i}=\alpha_{i}\quad(i=1,2,\dots n)$;

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
**唯一性**
设$V$中任一向量$\xi$可以由$V$的一组基$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$线性表出,即$\xi=x_{1}\varepsilon_{1}+x_{2}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots x_{n}\varepsilon_{n}$
由于线性映射保持线性关系不变,因此
$\mathcal{A}\xi=x_{1}\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{1}+\dots x_{n}\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{n}=x_{1}\mathcal{B}\varepsilon_{1}+\dots x_{n}\mathcal{B}\varepsilon_{n}=\mathcal{B}\xi$

**存在性**
设$\xi=\sum\limits_{i=1}^{n}x_{i}\varepsilon_{i}$,事实上,此线性映射就是:
$\mathcal{A}:\quad \begin{matrix}V\longrightarrow V'\\ \xi=\sum\limits_{i=1}^{n}x_{i}\varepsilon_{i}\longmapsto \sum\limits_{i=1}^{n}x_{i}\alpha_{i}\end{matrix}$
即$\mathcal{A}\xi=\sum\limits_{i=1}^{n}x_{i}\alpha_{i}$
$1^\circ$ 易证$\mathcal{A}$是线性映射
$2^\circ$ 再证$\mathcal{A}$满足$\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{i}=\alpha_{i},\quad(i=1,2,\dots n)$
由于$\varepsilon_{i}=0\varepsilon_{1}+\dots1\varepsilon_{i}+\dots0\varepsilon_{n},\quad i=1,2,\dots n$
所以$\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{i}=0\alpha_{1}+\dots1\alpha_{i}+\dots+0\alpha_{n}=\alpha_{i},\quad i=1,2,\dots n$

<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

### 1.3 线性映射的运算
><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:线性映射的运算</span>
> (以下涉及的线性空间都是域$F$上的)
>==加法== 设$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,定义$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$的和$\mathcal{A+B}$为$(\mathcal{A+B})(\alpha)=\mathcal{A}(\alpha)+\mathcal{B}(\alpha),\alpha\in V$,则线性映射的和还是线性映射,即$\mathcal{A+B}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$.
>**加法交换律** $\mathcal{A+B=B+A}$
>**加法结合律** $\mathcal{(A+B)+C=A+(B+C)}$
>**零元** $\mathcal{0}$是零映射,$\mathcal{A+0=A}$
>**负元** $-\mathcal{A}$是$\mathcal{A}$的负映射,$\mathcal{A+(-A)=0}$
>
>==数乘== 设$k\in F,\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,定义$k,\mathcal{A}$的数乘为$(k\mathcal{A})(\alpha)=k\mathcal{A}(\alpha),\forall\alpha\in V$,则线性映射的数乘还是线性映射,即$k\mathcal{A}\in Hom(V,V')$
>**一元** $1\cdot \mathcal{A}=\mathcal{A}$
>**结合律** $kl(\mathcal{A})=k(l\mathcal{A})$
>**分配律** $k(\mathcal{A+B})=k\mathcal{A}+k\mathcal{B},(k+l)\mathcal{A}=k\mathcal{A}+l\mathcal{A}$
>
>==乘法==  设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,W),\mathcal{B}\in \mathrm{Hom}(U,V)$,定义$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$的乘积$\mathcal{AB}$为$(\mathcal{AB})(\alpha)=\mathcal{A}(\mathcal{B}(\alpha)),\alpha\in V$,则线性映射的乘积还是线性映射,即$\mathcal{AB}\in \mathrm{Hom}(U,W)$.
>**结合律** $(\mathcal{AB})\mathcal{C}=\mathcal{A}(\mathcal{BC})$
>**分配律** $\mathcal{A}\mathcal{(B+C)}=\mathcal{AB+AC},\mathcal{(A+B)C=AC+BC}$
>**非交换性** 一般$\mathcal{AB\neq BA}$
>**单位变换** $\mathcal{E}$是单位变换,$\forall\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V)$,有$\mathcal{EA=AE=A}$
>
>==逆映射== 设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,若存在$\mathcal{A^{-1}}:V'\longrightarrow V,s.t.\mathcal{AA^{-1}}=\mathcal{E}_{V'},\mathcal{A^{-1}A}=\mathcal{E}_{V}$,则称$\mathcal{A^{-1}}$为$\mathcal{A}$的逆线性映射


>[!note] 
>设$V,V'$都是数域P上的线性空间,把$V$到$V'$的所有线性映射组成的集合记作$\mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$(或$\mathcal{L}(V,V')$);把$V$上所有线性变换组成的集合记作$\mathrm{Hom}(V)$(或$\mathcal{L}(V)$,或$\mathrm{End}(V)$)
>
>
>记$M_{m\times n}(P)$为数域$P$上所有$m\times n$矩阵全体的集合


>[!important] 
>$V,V'$都是域$F$上的线性空间,
>1) 对于从$V$到$V'$的所有线性映射组成的集合$\mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,如上定义加法和数乘,$\mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$构成域$F$上的线性空间.
>2) 对于$V$上的所有线性变换组成的集合$\mathrm{Hom}(V)$,如上定义加法和乘法,$\mathrm{Hom}(V)$构成幺环.此时称它为自同态环,记为$\mathrm{End}(V)$

> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:域上的代数」</span>
> 一个非空集合$A$如果定义了加法、乘法,亦即域$F$与$A$的数量乘法运算,并且$A$对于加法和数量乘法成为域$F$上的一个线性空间,$A$对于加法和乘法成为一个幺环,$A$的乘法和数乘满足$k(\alpha\beta)=(k\alpha)\beta=\alpha(k\beta)\quad \forall k\in F,\alpha,\beta\in A$.那么称$A$为域$F$上的一个代数,把线性空间$A$的维数称为代数$A$的维数
> 
> 显然,$\mathrm{Hom}(V)$是域$F$上的一个代数

### 1.4 特殊线性变换
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:投影变换」</span>
>设$V$是数域P上的一个线性空间,$U,W$是$V$的两个子空间,且$V=U\oplus W$.任取$\alpha\in V$,设$\alpha=\alpha_{1}+\alpha_{2},\alpha_{1}\in U,\alpha_{2}\in W$,令
>$\mathcal{P}_{U}:\quad \begin{matrix}V\longrightarrow V\\\alpha\longmapsto\alpha_{1}\end{matrix}$
>则$\mathcal{P}_{U}$是$V$上的一个线性变换.称$\mathcal{P}_{U}$是平行于$W$在$U$上的投影,它满足
>$\mathcal{P}_{U}(\alpha)=\begin{cases}\alpha,&\alpha\in U\\0,&\alpha\in W\end{cases}$
>满足上式的$V$上的线性变换是唯一的

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161127057.png)



> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:幂等变换」</span>
> 线性空间$V$上的线性变换$\mathcal{A}$如果满足$\mathcal{A}^2=\mathcal{A}$,那么称$\mathcal{A}$是幂等变换
> 
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:正交」</span>
> 线性空间$V$上的两个变换$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$如果满足$\mathcal{AB}=\mathcal{BA}=\mathcal{O}$,那么称$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$是正交的



><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:投影的特征性质</span>
>1)设$U,W$是域$F$上线性空间$V$的两个子空间,且$V=U\oplus W$,则平行于$W$在$U$上的投影$\mathcal{P}_{U}$,和平行于$U$在$W$上的投影$\mathcal{P}_{W}$是正交的幂等变换,且它们的和等于恒等变换
>2)设$V$是域$F$上的线性空间,$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$是$V$上的正交的幂等变换,且$\mathcal{A}+\mathcal{B}=\mathcal{I}$.则$V=\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}+\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{B}$,且$\mathcal{A}$是平行于$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{B}$在$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$上的投影,$\mathcal{B}$是平行于$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$在$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{B}$上的投影.

>[!note] 
>可扩展到多个两两正交的幂等变换的情形

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
1)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161129734.png)
2)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161130300.png)



> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:对合变换」</span>
> 域$F$上线性空间$V$上的线性变换$\mathcal{A}$如果满足$\mathcal{A}^2=\mathcal{I}$,则称$\mathcal{A}$是对合变换

>[!example] 
>![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506110920631.png)
>如图,定义几何空间$V$中$\alpha$关于平面$U$的镜面反射为$\mathcal{R}_{U}(\alpha)=\beta$
>而直线$W\perp U$,$W$是$V$的一个子空间,且$V=U\oplus W$,于是$\vec{OC}$是$\alpha$在投影$\mathcal{P}_{W}$下象,即$\mathcal{P}_{W}(\alpha)=\vec{OC}$
>$\mathcal{R}_{U}$是对合变换



> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:幂零变换」</span>
> 域$F$上线性空间$V$上的线性变换$\mathcal{A}$,如果存在正整数$l$使得$\mathcal{A}^l=\mathcal{O}$,那么称$\mathcal{A}$是幂零变换;使$\mathcal{A}^l=\mathcal{O}$成立的最小正整数$l$称为$\mathcal{A}$的幂零指数.

>[!example] 
>$R[x]_{n}$上的求导数$\mathcal{D}$是幂零指数为$n$的幂零变换


---

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
设$\mathcal{A}$是线性空间$V$中的一个线性变换.试证:如果$\mathcal{A}^{m-1}\alpha\neq0,\mathcal{A}^m\alpha=0(m\in \mathbb{N}^*)$,那么$\alpha,\mathcal{A}\boldsymbol{\alpha}\dots\mathcal{A}^{m-1}\boldsymbol{\alpha}$线性无关

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161152819.png)


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
设$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$是域$F$上线性空间$V$上的线性变换.证明:如果$\mathcal{AB}-\mathcal{BA}=\mathcal{I}$,那么$\mathcal{A}^k\mathcal{B}-\mathcal{B}\mathcal{A}^k=k\mathcal{A}^{k-1},\quad k\geqslant1$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161152731.png)


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
设$V$是域$F$上的线性空间,$\mathrm{char}F\neq2$.设$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$是$V$上的幂等变换,证明:
1)$\mathcal{A}+\mathcal{B}$是幂等变换当且仅当$\mathcal{AB}=\mathcal{BA}=\mathcal{O}$
2)如果$\mathcal{AB}=\mathcal{BA}$,那么$\mathcal{A}+\mathcal{B}-\mathcal{AB}$也是幂等变换
<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161704648.png)



## 2 线性映射的核与像
> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:核与像」</span>
> 域$F$上,设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,$V'$的零向量在$\mathcal{A}$下的原像集称为$\mathcal{A}$的核,记为$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}$或$\mathcal{A}^{-1}(0)$,即$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}=\{ \alpha\in V|\mathcal{A}\alpha=0' \}$
> $\mathcal{A}$的全体像组成的集合称为$\mathcal{A}$的像(也叫值域),记作$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$或$\mathcal{A}V$
> 
> $\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$的维数称为$\mathcal{A}$的<span style="background:#d2cbff">秩</span>;$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}$的维数称为$\mathcal{A}$的<span style="background:#d2cbff">零度</span>
> 
> ==🖇️Properties：==
> 1)设$\dim V=n,\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V),\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$是$V$的一组基,在这组基下$\mathcal{A}$的矩阵是$A$,则:
> 	1.1)$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}=L(\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{1},\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{2},\dots \mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{n})$
> 	1.2)$\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{A})=\mathrm{rank}(A)$
> 2)$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}$是$V$的一个子空间,$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$是$V'$的一个子空间
> 3)域$F$上,$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,则:
>	3.1)$\mathcal{A}$是单射当且仅当$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}=0$
>	3.2)$\mathcal{A}$是满射当且仅当$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}=V'$
>	3.3)$\mathcal{A}$是单射当且仅当$\mathcal{A}$是满射

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
1)
设$\xi$是$V$中的任一向量,可用基的线性组合表示为$\xi=x_{1}\varepsilon_{1}+x_{2}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots x_{n}\varepsilon_{n}$
于是$\mathcal{A}\xi=x_{1}\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{1}+x_{2}\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{2}+\dots x_{n}\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{n}$
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161723765.png)
2)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161723243.png)

3)
3.1)3.2)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161707401.png)
3.3)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161707598.png)


>[!attention] 
>$\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{1},\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{2},\dots \mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{n}$不一定是$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$的一组基,比如对于线性变换$\mathcal{D}(f)=f',\mathcal{D}\in \mathrm{Hom}(P[x]_{n})$,有$\mathcal{D}(1,x,x^2,\dots x^{n-1})=(0,1,2x, \dots(n-1)x^{n-2})$,显然$0,1,2x, \dots(n-1)x^{n-2}$不是一组基


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:核的商空间-象同构定理</span>
>域$F$上,$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,令$\sigma:\begin{matrix}V/\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}\longrightarrow\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}\\\alpha+\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}\longmapsto\mathcal{A}\alpha\end{matrix}$,则$\sigma$是同构映射,从而$V/\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}\cong\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161708441.png)

><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:秩-零度定理</span>
>域$F$上,$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,$V$是有限维的,则$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A},\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$都是有限维的,且$\dim(\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A})+\dim(\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A})=\dim(V)$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161709968.png)


><span style='font-family:汉仪劲楷简 Regular,Stem;font-style: normal;font-weight: bold;color: #242424;text-decoration: none;text-shadow: 1px 1px 1px #eeece1;font-size:1.5em;background-image: linear-gradient(to right, #92fe9d 0%, #00c9ff 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 29px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.68);padding:3px;'>Theorem:幂等变换等价投影</span>
>域$F$上,$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V)$.如果$\mathcal{A}$是$V$上的幂等变换,那么$V=\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}\oplus \mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}$,并且$\mathcal{A}$是平行于$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}$在$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$上的投影

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161726088.png)

>[!note] 
>此命题说明幂等变换是投影,而之前已经证明投影是幂等变换,因而两者等价.


> <span style='background-image: linear-gradient(120deg, #89f7fe 0%, #66a6ff 100%);font-size:1.5em;font-style:normal;padding:2px;font-family:方正龙爪简体;font-weight:bold;border-radius:0 10px 0 0;box-shadow: 2px 2px 5px 3px #ccc;'>「Definition:余核」</span>
> 设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,由于$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$是$V'$的子空间,那么就有商空间$V'/\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$,将其称为$\mathcal{A}$的余核,记为$\mathrm{Coker}\mathcal{A}$
> 
> ==🖇️Property：==
> $\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$,$\mathcal{A}$是满射当且仅当$\mathrm{Coker}\mathcal{A}=0$

>[!note] 
>核描述了解的自由度(齐次方程解空间),余核描述了非满射程度(解存在的约束条件)


---

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 1 </span>
证明:
1)
设$V,U,W$都是域$F$上的线性空间,且$V$是有限维的.设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,U),\mathcal{B}\in \mathrm{Hom}(U,W)$.试证:$\dim(\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{BA})\leqslant\dim(\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A})+\dim(\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{B})$
2)==Sylvester秩不等式==
设$V,U,W$都是域$F$上的线性空间,且$\dim V=n,\dim U=m$.设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,U),\mathcal{B}\in \mathrm{Hom}(U,W)$.则$\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{BA})\geqslant\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{A})+\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{B})-m$
3)==Frobenius秩不等式==
设$V,U,W,M$都是域$F$上的线性空间,且$V,U$都是有限维的.设$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,U),\mathcal{B}\in \mathrm{Hom}(U,W),\mathcal{C}\in \mathrm{Hom}(W,M)$.试证:$\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{CBA})\geqslant \mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{CB})+\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{BA})-\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{B})$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
1)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161730248.png)

2)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161731301.png)

3)
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161731380.png)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 2 </span>
设$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$都是域$F$上线性空间$V$上的幂等变换,证明:
1)$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$有相同的象当且仅当$\mathcal{AB}=\mathcal{B},\mathcal{BA}=\mathcal{A}$
2)$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$有相同的核当且仅当$\mathcal{AB}=\mathcal{A},\mathcal{BA}=\mathcal{B}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof1 :</span>

<span style='display: inline-block; width: 0.8em; height: 0.8em; background: #000; margin-left: 0.5em; vertical-align: middle; box-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.2); margin-left:90%'></span>

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 3 </span>
设$V,V'$都是域$F$上的线性空间,$\mathcal{A}\in \mathrm{Hom}(V,V')$.试证:存在直和分解$V=\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}\oplus W,V'=M\oplus N$,使得$W\cong M$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161734533.png)


<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 4 </span>
把域$F$看成是自身上的一个线性空间,试证:$F$上的非零线性变换一定是线性空间$F$到自身的一个同构映射

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161734190.png)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 5 </span>
判断下面定义的映射$\mathcal{A}:P^4\longrightarrow P^3$是不是线性映射.如果是,求$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A},\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A},\mathrm{Coker}\mathcal{A}$
$\mathcal{A}\begin{bmatrix*}x_{1}\\x_{2}\\x_{3}\\x_{4}\end{bmatrix*}=\begin{bmatrix*}x_{1}-3x_{2}+x_{3}-2x_{4}\\-x_{1}-11x_{2}+2x_{3}-5x_{4}\\3x_{1}+5x_{2}+x_{4}\end{bmatrix*}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161734342.png)

>[!note] 
>求出线性映射在一个基下的矩阵后,$\mathrm{Ker}\mathcal{A}$等于n元齐次方程组$AX=0$的解空间,$\mathrm{Im}\mathcal{A}$等于$A$的列空间

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 6 </span>
==线性变换可逆的充要条件(有限维)==
设$\mathcal{A}$是域$F$上n维线性空间$V$上的线性变换,那么以下命题等价:
0)$\mathcal{A}$可逆 
1)若$\varepsilon_{1},\varepsilon_{2},\dots\varepsilon_{n}$为$V$的一个基,则$\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{1},\mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{2},\dots \mathcal{A}\varepsilon_{n}$是$V$的一个基
2)对于任意$V$中的非零向量$\alpha$,有$\mathcal{A}\alpha\neq0$
3)若$V=V_{1}\oplus V_{2}$,则$V=\mathcal{A}V_{1}+\mathcal{A}V_{2}$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
1)

![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161739352.png)

![image.png](https://locus622.oss-cn-beijing.aliyuncs.com/img/202506161739732.png)

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(45deg, #93a5cf 0%, #e4efe9 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'> eg. 7 </span>
设$\mathcal{A},\mathcal{B}$都是域$F$上n维线性空间$V$上的线性变换,证明:如果$\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{AB})=\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{B})$,那么对于$V$上的任意线性变换$\mathcal{C}$,都有$\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{ABC})=\mathrm{rank}(\mathcal{BC})$

<span style='color:#434343;background-image: linear-gradient(-20deg, #e9defa 0%, #fbfcdb 100%);border-radius:7px;box-shadow: 1px 1px 30px 5px rgb(204, 204, 204, 0.52);font-family:Monotype Corsiva;font-size:2em;'>Proof :</span>
